This file is a merged representation of a subset of the codebase, containing specifically included files and files not matching ignore patterns, combined into a single document by Repomix.
The content has been processed where empty lines have been removed.

================================================================
File Summary
================================================================

Purpose:
--------
This file contains a packed representation of a subset of the repository's contents that is considered the most important context.
It is designed to be easily consumable by AI systems for analysis, code review,
or other automated processes.

File Format:
------------
The content is organized as follows:
1. This summary section
2. Repository information
3. Directory structure
4. Repository files (if enabled)
5. Multiple file entries, each consisting of:
  a. A separator line (================)
  b. The file path (File: path/to/file)
  c. Another separator line
  d. The full contents of the file
  e. A blank line

Usage Guidelines:
-----------------
- This file should be treated as read-only. Any changes should be made to the
  original repository files, not this packed version.
- When processing this file, use the file path to distinguish
  between different files in the repository.
- Be aware that this file may contain sensitive information. Handle it with
  the same level of security as you would the original repository.

Notes:
------
- Some files may have been excluded based on .gitignore rules and Repomix's configuration
- Binary files are not included in this packed representation. Please refer to the Repository Structure section for a complete list of file paths, including binary files
- Only files matching these patterns are included: **/*
- Files matching these patterns are excluded: .env, .env.*, *.key, *.pem, *.secret, secrets/, node_modules/, .venv/, venv/, __pycache__/, .pytest_cache/, .pycache-check/, pytest-cache-files-*/, .codex-tmp/, .git/, .vscode/, .idea/, dist/, build/, .astro/, .next/, coverage/, *.pyc, *.log, *.sqlite, *.sqlite3, *.db, *.db-journal, package-lock.json, yarn.lock, pnpm-lock.yaml, public/fonts/, public/images/, *.woff, *.woff2, *.ttf, *.png, *.jpg, *.jpeg, *.webp, *.svg, *.ico, repomix-output*.txt, repomix-output*.xml, repomix-*.txt, repomix-*.xml
- Files matching patterns in .gitignore are excluded
- Files matching default ignore patterns are excluded
- Empty lines have been removed from all files
- Files are sorted by Git change count (files with more changes are at the bottom)

`docs/EXECUTION_PLAN.md`\n5. `docs/AGENT_GUARDRAILS.md`\n6. `docs/AGENT_VISUAL_STANDARD.md`\n7. `docs/VALIDATION_RULES.md`\n8. `docs/maps/MAP_INDEX.md`\n9. `docs/maps/AGENT_TASK_TREE.md`\n\nSupporting source docs:\n\n- `project_blueprint.md`\n- the selected `profiles/<profile>.md`\n- the selected `request_types/<project_type>.md`\n- `docs/conductor/workflow.md`\n- `docs/conductor/security_policy.md`\n\n## Goal\n\nTurn the existing generated workspace into a convincing quick-start build for\nthe current request.\n\nThis is the launch base for the current active Нейроцех module:\n\n- scaffold already exists\n- request has already been normalized\n- architecture profile has already been resolved\n- the next job is to fill the first working version honestly and leave it ready for manager\n  publish\n\n## Current Module Rule\n\nOptimize for the current quick-start delivery flow first.\n\nDo not:\n\n- redesign the whole system for future modules\n- invent full production integrations that do not exist\n- fake completion of paid follow-up work\n- widen the scope beyond the current request without documenting it\n\nFuture growth should remain visible as extension seams, not as overbuilt code.\n\n## Astro Source Contract\n\n- Site source lives in `apps/site/src`.\n- Treat Astro components and `src/data/*.ts` files as the editable site source.\n- For landing requests, keep the starter content in `apps/site/src/data/landing.ts` and `apps/site/src/components/*.astro`.\n- Do not create hand-written `index.html`, `catalog.html`, or similar HTML source pages for the site.\n- HTML in `public-demo`, `dist`, `build`, `out`, or similar folders is publish output only.\n- If Astro build is unavailable in the current environment, record that fact in `docs/conductor/run_log.md`, but keep the source model in Astro.\n- For site work, compose pages from components and data instead of flattening the site into raw HTML.\n\n## UI Contracts v1\n\n- `ui_contracts` is the machine-readable UI contract layer between request metadata / visual context, scaffold, launch instruction, validator, validation report, and agent handoff.\n- In generated workspaces, treat `.botweaver/pipeline/spec.json` and `.botweaver/pipeline/launch-instruction.json` as the canonical handoff artifacts for resolved `ui_contracts`.\n- Current scaffold/validator v1 canonical defaults are:\n  - `drawer_position = left`\n  - `burger_animation = cross`\n  - `faq_icon = css-line`\n  - `card_grid_balance = count-4-compact`\n  - `hero_layout = from ui_contracts / visual context`\n  - requested color preset is applied through CSS variables (`--accent`, `--accent-strong`, `--accent-gradient`, `--accent-soft`, `--accent-glow`, etc.), not hardcoded blue values\n- Future-reserved values may exist in the contract surface, but the agent must not invent those variants until scaffold and validator explicitly support them.\n- If a future-reserved value appears, keep the output v1-safe and record the limitation in `docs/conductor/run_log.md` instead of silently expanding the scaffold contract.\n\n## What Success Looks Like\n\nA good result means:\n\n- the workspace no longer looks like a bare scaffold\n- the core user-facing path is visible and coherent\n- the result matches the niche, style, structure, and capabilities from the request\n- a publishable entrypoint exists for the quick-start build\n- the project stays safe to serve under `/demo/<public_request_id>/`\n\n## Quick-start Quality Bar\n\nThis is not a throwaway mockup. Treat the output as the first client-facing version.\n\nA successful quick-start build must:\n\n- look like a real client project, not a placeholder\n- have a concrete business vertical\n- communicate the offer in the first screen within 3 seconds\n- use relevant visuals, not only generic decorative assets\n- include a clear CTA and next step\n- avoid meta copy as the main commercial message\n- keep paid follow-up scope honest without making the page feel unfinished\n\nIf the request is too generic, choose one believable concrete vertical and record that choice in `run_log.md`.\nIf ecommerce already has a product category from the client, keep it as the source of truth. If it does not, choose one concrete ecommerce vertical and record both the choice and the reason in `run_log.md` using the exact markers:\n\n- `Chosen ecommerce vertical: <vertical>`\n- `Reason: <why this vertical was selected>`\n\n## Business Copy Policy\n\nThis policy applies to all frontend quick-start sites, not only landing pages.\n\n- Write visible business copy in a simpler, more neutral, and more concrete tone.\n- Start from the business, not from the website structure.\n- Before filling page data, build a niche-level business copy seed: what this business offers, who it helps, typical products/services/categories, CTA variants, benefit ideas, and FAQ topics.\n- Do not drift into abstract \"AI marketing\" phrasing when a plain business sentence would work.\n- If the brief is incomplete, write honestly and generally, but still write as a real niche business.\n- You may use typical niche categories or service directions when they are obvious from the brief.\n- Do not invent prices, addresses, years of experience, reviews, deadlines, guarantees, certificates, medical claims, or legal claims.\n- Do not write soft abstract phrases when a direct business sentence is clearer.\n- Do not make the main copy about cards, blocks, page structure, future editing, or how the site can be expanded later.\n\nAvoid these default phrases unless the brief explicitly justifies them:\n\n- `понятный путь`\n- `сценарий обращения`\n- `точечное обновление`\n- `собранный результат`\n- `удобная заявка на связь`\n- `без лишней суеты` as the main tone\n- `премиальный опыт`\n- `идеальный результат`\n- `экспертный подход`\n- `категории на виду`\n- `короткие карточки`\n- `быстрый контакт`\n- `каталог и заявка в один шаг`\n- `каталог и контакт собраны`\n- `сайт можно доработать`\n- `здесь можно добавить`\n\nReference tone examples:\n\n- `AnnaSW — салон красоты. Маникюр, брови, ресницы, макияж, укладка и уход по предварительной записи.`\n- `Пекарня у дома. Свежий хлеб, выпечка и десерты каждый день. Можно выбрать позиции и оставить заявку.`\n- `Каталог недвижимости. Квартиры, дома и коммерческие объекты. Поможем подобрать вариант и уточнить условия.`\n- `Горнолыжные товары из Европы. Одежда, маски, шлемы и аксессуары для катания. Подскажем наличие, размер и цену.`\n- `Автосервис. Диагностика, обслуживание и ремонт автомобиля по заявке. Можно описать задачу и уточнить формат работ.`\n\n## Business Copy Validator\n\nThe validator includes a warning check named `business-copy-meta-phrase-risk`.\n\nIt does not block demo publishing by itself, but it flags public text that still sounds like scaffold or owner-facing copy instead of business copy.\n\nIf the warning appears, rewrite the phrase as a direct business sentence about the client's offer, product category, service, booking, or next contact step.\n\nFor cards, use this shape:\n\n```text\nTitle: product / service / category name\nDescription sentence 1: what it is\nDescription sentence 2: who it fits / why it is useful\nCTA: order / clarify / book / sign up / leave request\n```\n\nAvoid using the forbidden scaffold/meta phrases in public HTML even when they are present in internal docs as examples of what not to write.\n\n## Project-Type Copy Adapters\n\n### Landing\n\n- Keep one main offer.\n- Hero copy should quickly answer: who this is, what it does, and how to contact or leave a request.\n- CTA should lead to the request form or contacts.\n- Do not overload the hero with explanations or abstract advantages.\n\n### Catalog / Store\n\n- Write through categories, products, selections, and clear choice paths.\n- If prices are missing, do not invent prices.\n- If exact products are missing, use real-looking categories or directions instead of fake SKUs.\n- Each card should answer: what it is, who it fits, and how to choose or leave a request.\n- Keep the page structure fixed by the selected catalog preset; do not invent detail pages or extra catalog modes.\n- The home page should preview 3-4 cards from the same catalog data that powers the catalog page.\n- The expanded preset uses About and Blog placeholder pages instead of detail or cases routes.\n\n### Services / Booking\n\n- Write through services, booking, consultation, and choosing time or format.\n- Duration, price, address, specialist, or guarantee may appear only when the brief provides them.\n- Service cards should stay simple: service name, short description, CTA.\n- Booking is a CTA or intent inside the catalog contract, not a separate booking engine or page mode.\n\n### Corporate Site\n\n- Write through the company, work directions, who it helps, and how to contact.\n- Keep the tone more neutral than a landing page.\n- Do not invent years of experience, clients, case counts, licenses, or partners.\n- If facts are limited, prefer neutral sections such as directions, process, contacts, and FAQ.\n\n## Niche Reference Examples\n\n- Beauty: `Студия ухода и макияжа по предварительной записи. Маникюр, брови, ресницы и макияж в одном месте.`\n- Food: `Кафе с основным меню, сезонными позициями и заказом навынос. Можно выбрать блюда и оставить заявку на бронь или заказ.`\n- Repair / services: `Ремонт и обслуживание техники с диагностикой и согласованием работ. Можно описать задачу и оставить заявку на связь.`\n- Fitness: `Студия тренировок для взрослых и подростков. Персональные и групповые занятия по записи.`\n- Tourism: `Локальные туры и поездки с понятными маршрутами и форматом участия. Можно выбрать направление и оставить заявку на консультацию.`\n\n## Quick-start Quality Baseline\n\nFor frontend-facing quick-start builds, keep this baseline by default:\n\n- use the local asset pool already included in the scaffold under `apps/<surface>/public/assets/demo/`\n- prefer the seeded publish bundle folders under `public-demo/assets/demo/` and `public-demo/data/` before creating parallel asset roots by hand\n- use `hero-desktop.webp` for desktop/tablet hero composition and `hero-mobile.webp` for mobile hero composition first; use `fs-hero-default.webp` and `fs-hero-mobile-default.webp` for `fullscreen-visual` hero defaults; keep `hero-1.webp` and `hero-mobile-1.webp` only as legacy fallback assets\n- catalog/product cards already have a scaffold-owned fallback image pool in `CatalogSection.astro`: `product-1.webp` through `product-4.webp`, then `category-1.webp` through `category-4.webp`; do not manually choose card images unless the brief or supplied assets give a better match\n- use `product-1.webp` through `product-8.webp`, `category-1.webp` through `category-4.webp`, and `gallery-1.webp` through `gallery-4.webp` first for product cards, category cards, gallery/proof, benefits, trust/proof, and catalog previews; keep `image-1.webp`, `image-2.webp`, and `image-3.webp` only as legacy fallback assets\n- preferred catalog/product card image ratio is 3:4, for example `900x1200` WebP; square `1:1` product images are acceptable when rendered with `fit='contain'`\n- do not search external image sources when the local pool already covers the task\n- do not replace a usable local asset with a CSS-only pseudo-image\n- if the request is ecommerce, make product/category cards concrete with image, price or price range, and a button-like CTA (`Button`, `.product-card__cta`, `.service-card__cta`, or equivalent), not a plain text link\n- do not use abstract care directions or service-group cards as the main ecommerce catalog if the brief already gives a product category\n- if `ui_contracts.hero_layout` resolves to immersive, treat it as a full-width visual hero/banner: let the background image span the viewport, keep only the eyebrow, H1, short lead, primary CTA, and optional secondary CTA inside the shared page content container, and move the canonical post-hero card surface immediately after it\n- for catalog/ecommerce home pages, a catalog preview directly after hero is a valid post-hero card surface; do not add a second visual-cards/catalog block only to satisfy validator\n- do not add a hero side panel, hero visual card, `hero__panel`, or `hero__content--split` in immersive mode\n- if branded placeholder art carries logo or text, do not crop it away with `object-fit: cover`\n- default visible client copy to Russian unless the request explicitly asks for another language\n- show at least one real visual asset in the first visible fold; prefer the included desktop/mobile hero pair or a visible card/image asset before leaving the page imageless\n- finish the page as a complete shell: header, hero, main sections, CTA, and footer\n- quick-start lead forms are visible stubs by default: on submit, show a clear message that the form is not connected yet; do not call CRM, Telegram, email, or `/api/demo/lead` unless the task explicitly asks for a real integration\n- if the request includes a catalog page or catalog section, show visible product/category cards in the HTML or a static fallback, or use safe dynamic render with reveal re-registration; JS-only rendering is enhancement, not the only source of the catalog\n- never leave the catalog as an empty mount point that only becomes real after JS data/template rendering\n- if catalog cards use `[data-demo-reveal]` or another pre-visible state, re-register newly inserted cards after each render pass; make initReveal idempotent or root-aware\n- do not rely on a one-time reveal observer that only sees the initial DOM when the catalog is rendered dynamically\n- on mobile, product/category cards should read as a horizontal swipe row or carousel instead of a long vertical stack\n- on mobile, catalog/product/visual card rows should use horizontal swipe with `overflow-x: auto` and `scroll-snap-type: x mandatory`; service, feature, trust, process, and FAQ-style cards may stack vertically when that reads cleaner\n- if the header uses in-page anchors, keep scrolling smooth\n- if the header has multiple links, provide a mobile burger/toggle pattern instead of leaving navigation raw on small screens\n- keep the mobile burger inside `Header.astro`; do not create a separate floating `mobile-nav-toggle` in `MainLayout.astro`\n- keep the mobile header to brand/logo + burger only; move the primary CTA into the drawer, hero, or first content section\n- `ui_contracts.burger_animation` is the source of truth for the burger pattern; scaffold/validator v1 supports only `cross`\n- burger must be a real button with `aria-label`, `aria-expanded`, and `aria-controls`, and the v1 `cross` animation should animate its lines into a close state through `[aria-expanded=\"true\"]`\n- `ui_contracts.drawer_position` is the source of truth for drawer placement; scaffold/validator supports `left` and `right`\n- default mobile drawer is a scaffold-owned fixed panel; it may open from the configured `left` or `right` side and must stay viewport-safe/full-height\n- Header and MobileDrawer are scaffold-owned UI primitives; do not rebuild the mobile drawer from scratch unless the task explicitly changes the UI contract\n- the scaffold drawer may include its own custom close control, but validator does not deep-check internal close mechanics\n- validator checks only the configured drawer side (`left` / `right`) and viewport/full-height safety\n- drawer CTA must stay width-safe with `width: 100%`, `max-width: 100%`, and `box-sizing: border-box`\n- `ui_contracts.card_grid_balance` is the source of truth for four-card desktop balance; scaffold/validator v1 supports `count-4-compact` (four compact cards in one desktop row, with mobile swipe rows for catalog/visual cards). Legacy `count-4-2x2` is normalized to `count-4-compact` and is not the canonical output wording.\n- add visual polish through lightweight CSS: transitions, opacity, layered surfaces, soft motion, and clear hover states\n- prefer the included `demo-ui-baseline.css` as a baseline source before inventing ad hoc motion tokens from scratch\n\n## Catalog Structure Contract\n\n- Starter catalog = Home + Catalog + Contacts.\n- Expanded catalog = Home + Catalog + About + Blog + Contacts.\n- The catalog page is the only full listing page.\n- The full catalog stays on `/catalog`.\n- Do not create a product/service/object detail page.\n- Do not create `/catalog/[slug]`.\n- Do not require a cases/reviews/results page for catalog requests.\n- On the home page for catalog requests, a catalog preview immediately after hero is valid and preferred.\n- Do not add a second visual-cards block or duplicate catalog preview on the home page just to satisfy validator.\n- Home preview cards may reuse the same product/category data that powers `/catalog`, but they should stay a preview rather than a second full listing.\n- On mobile, render catalog cards as a horizontal swipe row or carousel instead of a tall vertical stack.\n- If the expanded catalog includes a blog page, keep it as an honest placeholder for future SEO/content growth rather than fake published articles.\n\n## Style Direction\n\n- Resolve visual direction before layout polish and before the final hero treatment.\n- If the brief names a style, fill `STYLE_DIRECTION_MAP.md` first and let it decide the visual metaphor, section rhythm, card treatment, button treatment, typography mood, media usage, motion, and what to avoid.\n- `dark-cyber`: do not reduce it to a dark background plus green buttons; use a visual metaphor such as a neon route, techno sign, terminal, or club atmosphere, and vary the rhythm across hero-banner, strip, cards, proof-row, and form-block sections.\n- `clean-premium`: keep the page airy with thin lines, calm surfaces, and compact but refined CTA styling.\n- `playful-product`: use soft geometry, friendly blocks, and a lively rhythm without drifting into childish chaos.\n- `editorial-tech`: use larger type, magazine-like spacing, text-led sections, and quiet buttons with disciplined accents.\n- If the style is still unclear, choose the most honest neutral direction and record the assumption in the map notes.\n\n## Hero Rules\n\n- Hero layout source of truth is `ui_contracts.hero_layout`; if it is absent, follow the resolved visual context / `heroLayoutPreference`.\n- Do not switch the configured hero layout on your own or invent new hero families until scaffold/validator explicitly support them.\n- If `ui_contracts.hero_layout` resolves to immersive, keep it as one full-bleed visual hero/banner with the eyebrow, H1, short lead, primary CTA, and optional secondary CTA inside the shared content container.\n- The background image may span the available width, but the readable content must stay inside a centered page-width container.\n- Do not turn an immersive hero into a split hero, a side panel, or a small card next to text.\n- Keep the hero wide enough to dominate the first fold visually.\n- Keep the H1 short: usually 3-7 words and at most 1-2 lines.\n- Keep the hero lead to 7 words or fewer.\n- Use at most 2 CTAs in the hero.\n- Do not fill `hero.note` for landing pages by default. Use it only when the brief needs one precise constraint that cannot fit the lead.\n- Do not add hero trust chips, badges, or a trust row under the CTA by default. Move proof, reviews, numbers, and trust cues into a separate section unless the brief explicitly asks for them in the hero.\n- Do not overload the hero with badges, chips, or explanatory microcopy.\n- If overlay is used, it must sit on top of the large banner, not become a separate card.\n- If the user chose a цельное hero-изображение, let the image dominate visually.\n\n### Immersive Hero Geometry\n\nThis is a hard geometry contract, not optional style advice.\n\n- If `ui_contracts.hero_layout` resolves to immersive, the hero must start immediately after the header with no visible background gap from the main container.\n- If `main.site-main` has `padding-top`, add an explicit immersive override such as `.site-main--immersive { padding-top: 0; }`.\n- If the source can add a main modifier, prefer `site-main site-main--immersive` for pages that start with an immersive hero.\n- The immersive hero may be full-bleed, but readable content must stay inside a centered page-width container.\n- Do not place immersive hero inside a padded main wrapper that creates a top gap.\n- Do not add split hero columns, hero side panels, hero visual cards, `hero__panel`, `hero__visual`, or `hero__content--split` in immersive mode.\n- Do not fake immersive full-bleed with `width: 100vw` and `margin-left: calc(50% - 50vw)`.\n- On mobile, add or preserve an explicit `.hero.hero--immersive { padding-top: 0; }` rule if a general `.hero` rule could add top padding.\n- On mobile, immersive hero CTA buttons must remain compact and must not become full-width slabs by default.\n- Hero content must keep bottom-safe padding so CTA buttons do not slide under the overlapping page surface.\n\n### Hero To Content Transition\n\n- For immersive hero pages, place one full-width `.page-surface` immediately after the hero and add `.page-surface--overlap` when the page background should rise over the hero edge.\n- Keep the normal page-width container inside `.page-surface__inner`; the overlap belongs to the full-width surface, not to a narrow first section.\n- The visual effect should read as: the page background rises over the bottom of the hero and then the rest of the sections continue in a normal flow.\n- Do not bring back the legacy `landing-content landing-content--overlap` wrapper.\n- Do not implement the overlap through `.hero--immersive + .section::before` or a similar first-section pseudo-element hack.\n- `.page-surface.page-surface--overlap` must stay lightweight: no `border`, `box-shadow`, `backdrop-filter`, `filter: blur()`, or glass/card/sheet treatment with translucent `rgba(...)` / `hsla(...)` wrapper backgrounds.\n- Do not use polygon, zigzag, or `clip-path` cuts for the hero-to-content transition.\n- Keep the overlap mobile-safe: reduce the upward offset on small screens and preserve a clean normal content flow after the first section.\n\n## FAQ Rules\n\n- FAQ icon source of truth is `ui_contracts.faq_icon`; scaffold/validator v1 supports only `css-line`.\n- Future-reserved FAQ icon values such as `svg` or `chevron` must not be implemented ad hoc in v1.\n- Keep FAQ on native `<details>/<summary>` by default.\n- Add lightweight CSS polish: smooth answer reveal, summary hover/focus transition, disclosure icon animation, and marker rotation on `[open]`.\n- Do not use a raw text disclosure marker such as `content: \"+\"`.\n- Draw the disclosure icon with CSS lines, for example through `summary::after` with two `linear-gradient` strokes or an equivalent line-based icon treatment.\n- Focus states must stay visible and keyboard-friendly.\n- Do not add a heavy JS accordion or animation library for the default scaffold.\n- Keep FAQ answers short and concrete; do not turn the block into a long article.\n\n## Buttons\n\nThis is a hard geometry contract, not optional style advice.\n\n- Keep default buttons compact: min-height around 38-40px and never above 44px.\n- Keep default button padding around `0.55rem 0.85rem`.\n- Keep default button corners around 14-16px and never above 18px.\n- Reserve large CTA styling for the hero or final CTA only.\n- Do not use large hero-style CTA buttons in the footer or as the default across the page.\n- On light backgrounds, `.button--secondary` and `.button--ghost` must set an explicit readable dark text color such as `color: var(--text)`; do not leave white text on white or pale button surfaces.\n- Tap target height is not the same as full-width button. On mobile, do not make hero buttons `width: 100%` by default.\n- Hero buttons may wrap, but they should stay visually compact: use `width: auto`, `fit-content`, or a reasonable `max-width`.\n- Full-width buttons are allowed only inside mobile drawers, checkout/payment flows, or explicit form submit contexts.\n- Never use `.hero__actions .button { width: 100%; }` unless the request explicitly asks for full-width mobile CTAs.\n- If a full-width button is used intentionally, document the reason in `docs/conductor/run_log.md`.\n\n## Forms\n\n- Prefer a compact centered lead form on desktop by default, with the form card around 760-860px wide unless the brief clearly needs a wider operational form.\n- Keep mobile lead forms at 100% width.\n- Do not create split form, left aside, or checklist-aside in the default quick-start landing scaffold.\n- Do not set `leadForm.layout` or similar generated landing data to enable split form. Split form needs a future explicit metadata field and a separate contract update.\n- Do not use the weak pattern \"short copy on the left, large form on the right\".\n- If a lead form includes a topic, service, or product select, make that field span the full form grid row; do not make every field full-width on desktop.\n- If the selected architecture includes API, the default lead form must submit into the local demo API boundary instead of stopping at a frontend-only success stub.\n- Keep the API demo-safe: acknowledge or store the lead locally, without CRM, email, Telegram, or external delivery by default.\n\n## CSS Source Hygiene\n\n- Do not append a second design system at the bottom of `site.css`.\n- If visual direction changes, consolidate existing core selectors instead of stacking new conflicting rules below old ones.\n- Avoid duplicate core selector blocks for `:root`, `.button`, `.site-main`, `.site-header`, `.hero`, and `.hero--immersive`.\n- Prefer one canonical source for button geometry, hero geometry, layout width, and header spacing.\n- If a generated scaffold already has a button or hero system, edit that system in place instead of adding parallel selectors that override it accidentally.\n\n## CSS Performance Rules\n\nThe first version must avoid heavy visual effects that cause jank in browsers.\n\nRules:\n\n- do not use `backdrop-filter` broadly\n- do not combine `backdrop-filter` + large blur + large box-shadow on many cards\n- avoid `filter: blur()` on large fixed or scrolling layers\n- do not turn `.page-surface` or `.page-surface--overlap` into a glass/card/sheet wrapper with `border`, heavy shadow, `backdrop-filter`, blur, or translucent `rgba(...)` / `hsla(...)` backgrounds\n- keep shadows soft and limited\n- use static gradients, borders, opacity layers, and lightweight hover transitions instead\n- if glass effect is used, apply it only to 1-2 key surfaces, not every card\n- mobile and Yandex/Chromium-based browsers should scroll smoothly\n\n## Boundaries\n\n- work inside the existing scaffold\n- preserve the resolved service boundaries\n- keep business logic in the proper layer\n- prefer simple structures that can grow later\n- document known limitations instead of hiding them\n\n## What Not To Fake\n\nDo not fake:\n\n- real production integrations\n- completed admin systems\n- partner dashboards\n- deep role systems\n- hidden backend behavior with no real implementation\n\nIf the request implies larger future work, leave a clean seam and note it as\nfollow-up scope.\n\n## Workflow\n\n### 1. Inspect\n\nDescribe:\n\n- the actual scaffold state\n- whether the runtime workspace is writable without ownership repair\n- the selected profile and request type\n- the likely publishable entrypoint\n- the files and paths that will be touched\n- risks or missing pieces before implementation\n- do not use `git status` inside the generated runtime workspace as a decision tool; use the scaffold files and pipeline artifacts instead\n- do not spend time searching external image sources if the local asset pool already contains usable hero images\n\n### 2. Plan\n\nProvide:\n\n- implementation order\n- content and structure priorities\n- approved paths and denied paths\n- checks needed for a credible quick-start result\n\n### 3. Implement\n\nOnly after approval for bounded L2 work:\n\n- fill the visible product path\n- keep the implementation consistent with the current request\n- keep the visual baseline complete and client-facing, not just technically valid\n- update run or handoff notes as needed\n\n### 4. Verify\n\nAt the end confirm:\n\n- what visible quick-start path now exists\n- where the publishable entrypoint is\n- what remains paid follow-up scope\n- whether the quick-start build uses the local asset pool, footer, mobile nav, and motion baseline\n- whether the final visible copy follows the expected client language instead of falling back to English\n- what checks ran or were skipped\n\n## Final Rules\n\n- keep the quick-start build honest\n- keep the architecture expandable\n- keep the output publish-safe\n- do not mark the work as fully shipped production",

    "workflow_rules": "# Manual Conductor Workflow\n\nThis file defines the lifecycle of human-controlled implementation work.\n\nIt is the process layer.\n\nIt does not duplicate:\n\n- approval details from `approval_matrix.md`\n- autonomy details from `autonomy_levels.md`\n- security rules from `security_policy.md`\n\n## Default Operating Mode\n\nThe default mode is `L2` approved bounded implementation.\n\nThat means:\n\n- inspect and planning may happen first\n- file edits begin only after human approval of the task boundaries\n- deploy, merge, secret handling, and destructive actions stay manual unless\n  explicitly approved\n\n## Lifecycle\n\n1. Draft the task.\n2. Inspect the repository or generated workspace.\n3. Propose a bounded plan.\n4. Get human approval for L2 implementation.\n5. Implement only inside approved paths.\n6. Run the agreed checks.\n7. Update the run log.\n8. Hand off for review, publish, or the next owner.\n\n## Required Companion Docs\n\nEvery L2+ task should use:\n\n- `task_template.md`\n- `run_log_template.md`\n- `approval_matrix.md`\n- `autonomy_levels.md`\n- `security_policy.md`\n\n## Status Values\n\n- `draft`\n- `planned`\n- `approved`\n- `in_progress`\n- `verifying`\n- `blocked`\n- `done`\n\n## Rule\n\nIf approval boundaries are unclear, the task must stop before implementation.",

declare module 'astro:content' {
	export interface RenderResult {
		Content: import('astro/runtime/server/index.js').AstroComponentFactory;
		headings: import('astro').MarkdownHeading[];
		remarkPluginFrontmatter: Record<string, any>;
	}
	interface Render {
		'.md': Promise<RenderResult>;
	}
	export interface RenderedContent {
		html: string;
		metadata?: {
			imagePaths: Array<string>;
			[key: string]: unknown;
		};
	}
	type Flatten<T> = T extends { [K: string]: infer U } ? U : never;
	export type CollectionKey = keyof DataEntryMap;
	export type CollectionEntry<C extends CollectionKey> = Flatten<DataEntryMap[C]>;
	type AllValuesOf<T> = T extends any ? T[keyof T] : never;
	export type ReferenceDataEntry<
		C extends CollectionKey,
		E extends keyof DataEntryMap[C] = string,
	> = {
		collection: C;
		id: E;
	};
	export type ReferenceLiveEntry<C extends keyof LiveContentConfig['collections']> = {
		collection: C;
		id: string;
	};
	export function getCollection<C extends keyof DataEntryMap, E extends CollectionEntry<C>>(
		collection: C,
		filter?: (entry: CollectionEntry<C>) => entry is E,
	): Promise<E[]>;
	export function getCollection<C extends keyof DataEntryMap>(
		collection: C,
		filter?: (entry: CollectionEntry<C>) => unknown,
	): Promise<CollectionEntry<C>[]>;
	export function getLiveCollection<C extends keyof LiveContentConfig['collections']>(
		collection: C,
		filter?: LiveLoaderCollectionFilterType<C>,
	): Promise<
		import('astro').LiveDataCollectionResult<LiveLoaderDataType<C>, LiveLoaderErrorType<C>>
	>;
	export function getEntry<
		C extends keyof DataEntryMap,
		E extends keyof DataEntryMap[C] | (string & {}),
	>(
		entry: ReferenceDataEntry<C, E>,
	): E extends keyof DataEntryMap[C]
		? Promise<DataEntryMap[C][E]>
		: Promise<CollectionEntry<C> | undefined>;
	export function getEntry<
		C extends keyof DataEntryMap,
		E extends keyof DataEntryMap[C] | (string & {}),
	>(
		collection: C,
		id: E,
	): E extends keyof DataEntryMap[C]
		? string extends keyof DataEntryMap[C]
			? Promise<DataEntryMap[C][E]> | undefined
			: Promise<DataEntryMap[C][E]>
		: Promise<CollectionEntry<C> | undefined>;
	export function getLiveEntry<C extends keyof LiveContentConfig['collections']>(
		collection: C,
		filter: string | LiveLoaderEntryFilterType<C>,
	): Promise<import('astro').LiveDataEntryResult<LiveLoaderDataType<C>, LiveLoaderErrorType<C>>>;
	/** Resolve an array of entry references from the same collection */
	export function getEntries<C extends keyof DataEntryMap>(
		entries: ReferenceDataEntry<C, keyof DataEntryMap[C]>[],
	): Promise<CollectionEntry<C>[]>;
	export function render<C extends keyof DataEntryMap>(
		entry: DataEntryMap[C][string],
	): Promise<RenderResult>;
	export function reference<
		C extends
			| keyof DataEntryMap
			// Allow generic `string` to avoid excessive type errors in the config
			// if `dev` is not running to update as you edit.
			// Invalid collection names will be caught at build time.
			| (string & {}),
	>(
		collection: C,
	): import('astro/zod').ZodPipe<
		import('astro/zod').ZodString,
		import('astro/zod').ZodTransform<
			C extends keyof DataEntryMap
				? {
						collection: C;
						id: string;
					}
				: never,
			string
		>
	>;
	type ReturnTypeOrOriginal<T> = T extends (...args: any[]) => infer R ? R : T;
	type InferEntrySchema<C extends keyof DataEntryMap> = import('astro/zod').infer<
		ReturnTypeOrOriginal<Required<ContentConfig['collections'][C]>['schema']>
	>;
	type ExtractLoaderConfig<T> = T extends { loader: infer L } ? L : never;
	type InferLoaderSchema<
		C extends keyof DataEntryMap,
		L = ExtractLoaderConfig<ContentConfig['collections'][C]>,
	> = L extends { schema: import('astro/zod').ZodSchema }
		? import('astro/zod').infer<L['schema']>
		: any;
	type DataEntryMap = {
	};
	type ExtractLoaderTypes<T> = T extends import('astro/loaders').LiveLoader<
		infer TData,
		infer TEntryFilter,
		infer TCollectionFilter,
		infer TError
	>
		? { data: TData; entryFilter: TEntryFilter; collectionFilter: TCollectionFilter; error: TError }
		: { data: never; entryFilter: never; collectionFilter: never; error: never };
	type ExtractEntryFilterType<T> = ExtractLoaderTypes<T>['entryFilter'];
	type ExtractCollectionFilterType<T> = ExtractLoaderTypes<T>['collectionFilter'];
	type ExtractErrorType<T> = ExtractLoaderTypes<T>['error'];
	type ExtractDataType<T> = ExtractLoaderTypes<T>['data'];
	type LiveLoaderDataType<C extends keyof LiveContentConfig['collections']> =
		LiveContentConfig['collections'][C]['schema'] extends undefined
			? ExtractDataType<LiveContentConfig['collections'][C]['loader']>
			: import('astro/zod').infer<
					Exclude<LiveContentConfig['collections'][C]['schema'], undefined>
				>;
	type LiveLoaderEntryFilterType<C extends keyof LiveContentConfig['collections']> =
		ExtractEntryFilterType<LiveContentConfig['collections'][C]['loader']>;
	type LiveLoaderCollectionFilterType<C extends keyof LiveContentConfig['collections']> =
		ExtractCollectionFilterType<LiveContentConfig['collections'][C]['loader']>;
	type LiveLoaderErrorType<C extends keyof LiveContentConfig['collections']> = ExtractErrorType<
		LiveContentConfig['collections'][C]['loader']
	>;
	export type ContentConfig = never;
	export type LiveContentConfig = never;

================
File: apps/site/scripts/copy-demo-output.mjs
================
import { cp, mkdir, readdir, rm } from 'node:fs/promises';
import path from 'node:path';

const SITE_DIR = process.cwd();
const DIST_DIR = path.join(SITE_DIR, 'dist');
const PROJECT_ROOT = path.resolve(SITE_DIR, '..', '..');
const PUBLIC_DEMO_DIR = path.join(PROJECT_ROOT, 'public-demo');
const PRESERVED_DEMO_ASSETS_DIR = path.join(PUBLIC_DEMO_DIR, 'assets', 'demo');
const PRESERVED_DATA_DIR = path.join(PUBLIC_DEMO_DIR, 'data');

async function exists(filePath) {
  try {
    await readdir(filePath);
    return true;
  } catch {
    return false;
  }
}

async function removePublicDemoExceptDemoAssets() {
  await mkdir(PRESERVED_DEMO_ASSETS_DIR, { recursive: true });
  await mkdir(PRESERVED_DATA_DIR, { recursive: true });

  let entries = [];
  try {
    entries = await readdir(PUBLIC_DEMO_DIR, { withFileTypes: true });
  } catch {
    return;
  }

  for (const entry of entries) {
    const fullPath = path.join(PUBLIC_DEMO_DIR, entry.name);

    if (entry.name === 'data') {
      continue;
    }

    if (entry.name === 'assets') {
      const assetEntries = await readdir(fullPath, { withFileTypes: true }).catch(() => []);
      for (const assetEntry of assetEntries) {
        if (assetEntry.name === 'demo') continue;
        await rm(path.join(fullPath, assetEntry.name), { recursive: true, force: true });
      }
      continue;
    }

    await rm(fullPath, { recursive: true, force: true });
  }
}

async function main() {
  if (!(await exists(DIST_DIR))) {
    throw new Error(`Astro dist directory not found: ${DIST_DIR}`);
  }

  await mkdir(PUBLIC_DEMO_DIR, { recursive: true });
  await removePublicDemoExceptDemoAssets();
  await cp(DIST_DIR, PUBLIC_DEMO_DIR, { recursive: true, force: true });

  console.log(`Copied Astro dist to ${path.relative(PROJECT_ROOT, PUBLIC_DEMO_DIR) || PUBLIC_DEMO_DIR}`);
}

main().catch((error) => {
  console.error(error instanceof Error ? error.stack || error.message : String(error));
  process.exitCode = 1;
});

================
File: apps/site/scripts/fix-relative-assets.mjs
================
import { readFile, readdir, stat, writeFile } from 'node:fs/promises';
import path from 'node:path';

const SITE_DIR = process.cwd();
const ROOTS = [
  path.join(SITE_DIR, 'dist'),
  path.resolve(SITE_DIR, '..', '..', 'public-demo'),
];

const LOCAL_ATTRS = /(?:href|src|poster|action|data-src|data-href|srcset)=(["'])([^"']*)\1/gi;

function isExternalUrl(value) {
  return /^(?:[a-z][a-z0-9+.-]*:|\/\/|#|\?|\.\/|\.\.\/|data:|mailto:|tel:|javascript:)/i.test(value);
}

function depthPrefix(depth) {
  return depth > 0 ? '../'.repeat(depth) : './';
}

function rewriteLocalUrl(value, prefix) {
  const trimmed = value.trim();
  if (!trimmed || isExternalUrl(trimmed)) return value;

  const normalized = trimmed.replace(/^\.\//, '').replace(/^\/+/, '');
  if (!normalized) return prefix;

  return `${prefix}${normalized}`;
}

function rewriteSrcset(value, prefix) {
  return value
    .split(',')
    .map((entry) => {
      const trimmed = entry.trim();
      if (!trimmed) return trimmed;

      const parts = trimmed.split(/\s+/);
      const url = parts.shift();
      if (!url) return trimmed;

      parts.unshift(rewriteLocalUrl(url, prefix));
      return parts.join(' ');
    })
    .join(', ');
}

function rewriteHtml(content, depth) {
  const prefix = depthPrefix(depth);

  return content.replace(LOCAL_ATTRS, (full, quote, value) => {
    const attrName = (full.match(/^([a-z-]+)/i) || [])[1]?.toLowerCase() ?? '';
    const rewritten = attrName === 'srcset'
      ? rewriteSrcset(value, prefix)
      : rewriteLocalUrl(value, prefix);

    return `${attrName || 'href'}=${quote}${rewritten}${quote}`;
  });
}

async function walk(directory, files = []) {
  const entries = await readdir(directory, { withFileTypes: true });

  for (const entry of entries) {
    const fullPath = path.join(directory, entry.name);

    if (entry.isDirectory()) {
      await walk(fullPath, files);
      continue;
    }

    if (entry.isFile() && entry.name.endsWith('.html')) {
      files.push(fullPath);
    }
  }

  return files;
}

async function main() {
  const rewritten = [];

  for (const root of ROOTS) {
    try {
      const rootStat = await stat(root);
      if (!rootStat.isDirectory()) continue;
    } catch {
      continue;
    }

    for (const filePath of await walk(root)) {
      const raw = await readFile(filePath, 'utf8');
      const depth = path.relative(root, filePath).split(path.sep).slice(0, -1).length;
      const updated = rewriteHtml(raw, depth);

      if (updated !== raw) {
        await writeFile(filePath, updated, 'utf8');
        rewritten.push(path.relative(process.cwd(), filePath));
      }
    }
  }

  if (rewritten.length > 0) {
    console.log(`Fixed relative asset links in ${rewritten.length} HTML file(s).`);
  }
}

main().catch((error) => {
  console.error(error instanceof Error ? error.stack || error.message : String(error));
  process.exitCode = 1;
});

import { componentVariantMarkers } from '../data/site';

interface Props {
  href?: string;
  variant?: 'primary' | 'secondary' | 'ghost';
  type?: 'button' | 'submit' | 'reset';
  class?: string;
  [key: string]: unknown;
}

const { href, variant = 'primary', type = 'button', class: className = '', ...rest } = Astro.props;
const Tag = href ? 'a' : 'button';
const buttonVariantMarker = componentVariantMarkers.button;
const classes = ['button', `button--${variant}`, buttonVariantMarker.className, className].filter(Boolean).join(' ');
---
<Tag class={classes} href={href} type={href ? undefined : type} {...rest} {...buttonVariantMarker.dataAttrs}>
  <slot />
</Tag>

File: apps/site/src/components/Footer.astro

import { hasLeadForm, siteMeta } from '../data/site';

interface Props {
  navigation: readonly { readonly label: string; readonly href: string }[];
  links: readonly { readonly label: string; readonly href: string; readonly value: string }[];
}

const { navigation, links } = Astro.props;

function toLocalSiteHref(href: string): string {
  if (!href.startsWith('/')) return href;

  const trimmed = href.replace(/^\/+/, '');
  const segments = Astro.url.pathname.split('/').filter(Boolean);
  const prefix = '../'.repeat(segments.length);
  if (!trimmed) {
    return prefix || './';
  }
  return `${prefix}${trimmed}`;
}
---
<footer class="site-footer">
  <div class="site-footer__inner">
    <div class="site-footer__brand">
      <a href={toLocalSiteHref('/')}>{siteMeta.name}</a>
      {siteMeta.description && <p>{siteMeta.description}</p>}
    </div>

    <nav class="site-footer__nav" aria-label="Навигация в подвале">
      {navigation.map((item) => <a href={toLocalSiteHref(item.href)}>{item.label}</a>)}
    </nav>

    {links.length > 0 && (
      <div class="site-footer__links" aria-label="Контакты">
        {links.map((item) => (
          <a href={item.href}>
            <span>{item.label}</span>
            <strong>{item.value}</strong>
          </a>
        ))}
      </div>
    )}
    {hasLeadForm && (
      <div class="site-footer__legal">
        <a href={toLocalSiteHref('/privacy')}>Политика конфиденциальности</a>
      </div>
    )}
  </div>
</footer>

import Button from './Button.astro';
import { componentVariantMarkers, siteMeta } from '../data/site';

interface Props {
  navigation: readonly { readonly label: string; readonly href: string }[];
  cta: { readonly label: string; readonly href: string };
}

const { navigation, cta } = Astro.props;
const headerVariant = componentVariantMarkers.header;
const burgerVariant = componentVariantMarkers.burger;
const transparentScrollMode = headerVariant.variant === 'transparent-scroll';
const brandName = siteMeta.name.trim();
const brandInitials = brandName ? brandName.charAt(0).toUpperCase() : 'NC';
const headerClassName = [
  'site-header',
  headerVariant.className,
].filter(Boolean).join(' ');
const burgerClassName = ['site-header__burger', burgerVariant.className].filter(Boolean).join(' ');
---
<header
  id="main-header"
  class={headerClassName}
  data-header-scrolled={transparentScrollMode ? 'false' : undefined}
  {...headerVariant.dataAttrs}
>
  <div class="site-header__inner">
    <a class="site-brand" href="/" aria-label={siteMeta.name}>
      <span class="site-brand__mark" aria-hidden="true">{brandInitials}</span>
      <span class="site-brand__text">{siteMeta.name}</span>
    </a>

    <nav class="site-nav" aria-label="Основная навигация">
      {navigation.map((item) => <a href={item.href}>{item.label}</a>)}
    </nav>

    <Button href={cta.href} class="site-header__cta">{cta.label}</Button>

    <button class={burgerClassName} type="button" aria-controls="mobile-menu" aria-expanded="false" aria-label="Открыть меню" data-drawer-toggle {...burgerVariant.dataAttrs}>
      <span class="burger-line" aria-hidden="true"></span>
      <span class="burger-line" aria-hidden="true"></span>
      <span class="burger-line" aria-hidden="true"></span>
    </button>
  </div>
</header>
{transparentScrollMode && (
  <script>
    const header = document.getElementById('main-header');
    let headerFrameRequested = false;

    const syncHeaderState = () => {
      headerFrameRequested = false;

      if (!(header instanceof HTMLElement)) {
        return;
      }

      const shouldUseScrolledState = window.scrollY > 24;
      header.dataset.headerScrolled = shouldUseScrolledState ? 'true' : 'false';
    };

    const requestHeaderStateSync = () => {
      if (headerFrameRequested) {
        return;
      }

      headerFrameRequested = true;
      window.requestAnimationFrame(syncHeaderState);
    };

    window.addEventListener('scroll', requestHeaderStateSync, { passive: true });
    syncHeaderState();
  </script>
)}

import Button from './Button.astro';
import { componentVariantMarkers, leadFormTransport } from '../data/site';

interface Props {
  title: string;
  lead: string;
  topics?: readonly string[];
}

const { title, lead, topics = [] } = Astro.props;
const topicOptions = topics.map((item) => item.trim()).filter(Boolean).slice(0, 8);
const leadFormVariant = componentVariantMarkers.leadForm;
const sectionVariant = componentVariantMarkers.section;
const leadFormClassName = ['lead-form', sectionVariant.className, 'lead-form--compact', leadFormVariant.className].filter(Boolean).join(' ');
---
<section class={leadFormClassName} data-form-layout="compact" id="contact" aria-labelledby="lead-form-title" {...sectionVariant.dataAttrs} {...leadFormVariant.dataAttrs}>
  <div class="lead-form__header">
    <p class="section-heading__eyebrow">Заявка</p>
    <h2 id="lead-form-title">{title}</h2>
    <p class="lead-form__lead">{lead}</p>
  </div>

  <form
    class="lead-form__form"
    data-lead-form
    data-api-mode={leadFormTransport.mode}
    data-api-endpoint={leadFormTransport.endpoint}
    data-loading-message={leadFormTransport.loadingMessage}
    data-success-message={leadFormTransport.successMessage}
    data-local-success-message={leadFormTransport.localSuccessMessage}
    data-error-message={leadFormTransport.errorMessage}
    novalidate
  >
    <div class="lead-form__fields">
      <label class="lead-form__field">
        <span>Ваше имя</span>
        <input type="text" name="name" autocomplete="name" required />
      </label>

      <label class="lead-form__field">
        <span>Телефон или Telegram</span>
        <input type="text" name="contact" autocomplete="tel" required />
      </label>

      {topicOptions.length > 0 && (
        <label class="lead-form__field lead-form__field--topic">
          <span>Тема заявки</span>
          <select name="topic" required>
            <option value="">Выберите направление</option>
            {topicOptions.map((topic) => <option value={topic}>{topic}</option>)}
          </select>
        </label>
      )}

      <label class="lead-form__field lead-form__field--message">
        <span>Коротко опишите задачу</span>
        <textarea name="message" rows="4" required></textarea>
      </label>
    </div>

    <p class="lead-form__privacy">Нажимая кнопку, вы соглашаетесь на обработку данных для связи по заявке.</p>
    <p class="lead-form__status" data-form-status aria-live="polite"></p>
    <Button type="submit" class="lead-form__submit">Отправить заявку</Button>
  </form>

  <script>
    const forms = document.querySelectorAll('[data-lead-form]');

    forms.forEach((form) => {
      if (!(form instanceof HTMLFormElement)) return;

      const status = form.querySelector<HTMLElement>('[data-form-status]');
      const submit = form.querySelector<HTMLButtonElement>('button[type="submit"]');
      const defaultSubmitLabel = submit instanceof HTMLButtonElement ? submit.textContent || '' : '';
      const loadingMessage = form.dataset.loadingMessage || 'Проверяем форму…';
      const stubMessage =
        form.dataset.localSuccessMessage ||
        form.dataset.successMessage ||
        'Форма пока не подключена. Свяжитесь с владельцем сайта удобным способом.';
      const invalidMessage = 'Проверьте обязательные поля.';

      type LeadFormState = 'idle' | 'loading' | 'success' | 'error';

      const setStatus = (state: LeadFormState, message: string) => {
        form.dataset.state = state;
        form.setAttribute('aria-busy', state === 'loading' ? 'true' : 'false');

        if (status instanceof HTMLElement) {
          status.textContent = message;
        }
      };

      const setSubmitLoading = (loading: boolean) => {
        if (submit instanceof HTMLButtonElement) {
          submit.disabled = loading;
          submit.dataset.loading = loading ? 'true' : 'false';
        }
      };

      form.addEventListener('submit', (event) => {
        event.preventDefault();

        if (!form.checkValidity()) {
          setSubmitLoading(false);
          setStatus('error', invalidMessage);
          form.reportValidity();
          return;
        }

        setSubmitLoading(true);
        setStatus('loading', loadingMessage);

        setStatus('success', stubMessage);
        form.reset();
        setSubmitLoading(false);
        if (submit instanceof HTMLButtonElement) {
          submit.textContent = defaultSubmitLabel;
        }
      });
    });
  </script>
</section>

File: apps/site/src/components/MobileDrawer.astro
================
---
import Button from './Button.astro';
import { componentVariantMarkers, siteMeta } from '../data/site';

interface Props {
  navigation: readonly { readonly label: string; readonly href: string }[];
  cta: { readonly label: string; readonly href: string };
  position?: 'left' | 'right';
}

const { navigation, cta, position = 'left' } = Astro.props;
const drawerVariant = componentVariantMarkers.drawer;
const drawerPosition: 'left' | 'right' = position === 'right' ? 'right' : 'left';
const drawerClassName = ['mobile-drawer', `mobile-drawer--${drawerPosition}`].filter(Boolean).join(' ');
---
<div
  class={drawerClassName}
  id="mobile-menu"
  aria-hidden="true"
  data-mobile-drawer
  data-drawer-position={drawerPosition}
  {...drawerVariant.dataAttrs}
>
  <button class="mobile-drawer__scrim" type="button" aria-label="Закрыть меню" data-drawer-close></button>

  <aside class="mobile-drawer__panel" role="dialog" aria-label="Меню">
    <div class="mobile-drawer__top">
      <div class="mobile-drawer__brand">{siteMeta.name}</div>

      <button class="mobile-drawer__close" type="button" aria-label="Закрыть меню" data-drawer-close>
        <span class="mobile-drawer__close-line" aria-hidden="true"></span>
        <span class="mobile-drawer__close-line" aria-hidden="true"></span>
      </button>
    </div>

    <nav class="mobile-drawer__nav">
      {navigation.map((item) => <a href={item.href} data-drawer-close>{item.label}</a>)}
    </nav>

    <Button href={cta.href} class="mobile-drawer__cta">{cta.label}</Button>
  </aside>
</div>

<script>
  const drawer = document.querySelector('[data-mobile-drawer]');
  const toggles = document.querySelectorAll('[data-drawer-toggle]');
  const closeTargets = document.querySelectorAll('[data-drawer-close]');

  if (drawer instanceof HTMLElement) {
    const closeDirection = drawer.dataset.drawerPosition === 'right' ? 'right' : 'left';

    const setState = (open: boolean) => {
      drawer.setAttribute('data-open', open ? 'true' : 'false');
      drawer.setAttribute('aria-hidden', open ? 'false' : 'true');
      document.documentElement.classList.toggle('drawer-open', open);

      toggles.forEach((button) => {
        if (button instanceof HTMLButtonElement) {
          button.setAttribute('aria-expanded', open ? 'true' : 'false');
        }
      });
    };

    toggles.forEach((button) => {
      if (button instanceof HTMLButtonElement) {
        button.addEventListener('click', () => {
          setState(drawer.getAttribute('data-open') !== 'true');
        });
      }
    });

    closeTargets.forEach((target) => target.addEventListener('click', () => setState(false)));
    window.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => event.key === 'Escape' && setState(false));

    const panel = drawer.querySelector('.mobile-drawer__panel');
    let touchStartX = 0;
    let touchStartY = 0;

    if (panel instanceof HTMLElement) {
      panel.addEventListener('touchstart', (event) => {
        const touch = event.touches[0];
        if (!touch) return;

        touchStartX = touch.clientX;
        touchStartY = touch.clientY;
      }, { passive: true });

      panel.addEventListener('touchend', (event) => {
        const touch = event.changedTouches[0];
        if (!touch) return;

        const deltaX = touch.clientX - touchStartX;
        const deltaY = touch.clientY - touchStartY;

        const isHorizontalSwipe = Math.abs(deltaX) > 48 && Math.abs(deltaX) > Math.abs(deltaY) * 1.4;
        const isClosingSwipe = closeDirection === 'right' ? deltaX > 0 : deltaX < 0;

        if (isHorizontalSwipe && isClosingSwipe) {
          setState(false);
        }
      }, { passive: true });
    }
  }
</script>

import { clientBrief } from './client-brief';
const fallbackName =
  clientBrief.companyName.trim() ||
  clientBrief.businessDescription.trim() ||
  clientBrief.ecommerceProductCategory.trim() ||
  clientBrief.nicheDetail.trim() ||
  clientBrief.niche.trim() ||
  'Ваш проект';
const styleShapePresetMap = {
  'dark-cyber': 'sharp',
  'clean-premium': 'premium',
  'corporate-professional': 'premium',
  'playful-product': 'rounded',
  'playful-creative': 'rounded',
  'editorial-tech': 'premium',
} as const;
function normalizeShapePreset(value: string): '' | 'rounded' | 'sharp' | 'premium' {
  const normalized = value.trim().toLowerCase().replace(/_/g, '-');
  if (normalized === 'rounded' || normalized === 'sharp' || normalized === 'premium') {
    return normalized;
  }
  return '';
}
function getShapePresetForStyle(styleId: string): 'rounded' | 'sharp' | 'premium' {
  const normalizedStyleId = styleId.trim().toLowerCase().replace(/_/g, '-');
  return styleShapePresetMap[normalizedStyleId as keyof typeof styleShapePresetMap] ?? 'premium';
}
const resolvedShapePreset = normalizeShapePreset(clientBrief.shapePreset) || getShapePresetForStyle(clientBrief.style);
export const componentVariantMarkers = {
  "header": {

import Footer from '../components/Footer.astro';
import Header from '../components/Header.astro';
import MobileDrawer from '../components/MobileDrawer.astro';
import { footerLinks, navigation, siteMeta } from '../data/site';
import '../styles/site.css';
import '../styles/visual-tokens.css';

interface Props {
  title?: string;
  description?: string;
  immersive?: boolean;
}

const { title = siteMeta.title, description = siteMeta.description, immersive = false } = Astro.props;
---
<!doctype html>
<html lang="ru">
  <head>
    <meta charset="utf-8" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1" />
    <title>{title}</title>
    <meta name="description" content={description} />
  </head>
  <body data-shape-preset={siteMeta.shapePreset}>
    <Header navigation={navigation} cta={siteMeta.primaryCta} />
    <MobileDrawer navigation={navigation} cta={siteMeta.primaryCta} position={siteMeta.drawerPosition} />
    <main class:list={['site-main', immersive && 'site-main--immersive']}>
      <slot />
    </main>
    <Footer navigation={navigation} links={footerLinks} />
  </body>
</html>

import MainLayout from '../layouts/MainLayout.astro';
import Hero from '../components/Hero.astro';
import VisualCardsSection from '../components/VisualCardsSection.astro';
import ServicesSection from '../components/ServicesSection.astro';
import BenefitsSection from '../components/BenefitsSection.astro';
import TrustProof from '../components/TrustProof.astro';
import ProcessSection from '../components/ProcessSection.astro';
import Faq from '../components/Faq.astro';
import LeadForm from '../components/LeadForm.astro';
import { clientBrief } from '../data/client-brief';
import { benefits, faq, hero, landingContentStatus, leadForm, services, process, trustProof, visualCards } from '../data/landing';
import { componentVariantMarkers, siteMeta } from '../data/site';

type HeroLayoutPreference = 'split' | 'immersive' | 'fullscreen-visual';

const isBusinessContentReady = (landingContentStatus as string) === 'filled';
const hasHero = Boolean(hero && hero.title.trim() && hero.lead.trim());
const hasVisualCards = visualCards.title.trim().length > 0 && visualCards.items.length >= 3;
const hasServices = services.title.trim().length > 0 && services.items.length > 0;
const hasBenefits = benefits.title.trim().length > 0 && benefits.items.length > 0;
const hasTrustProof = trustProof.title.trim().length > 0 && trustProof.items.length > 0;
const hasProcess = process.title.trim().length > 0 && process.steps.length > 0;
const hasFaq = faq.title.trim().length > 0 && faq.items.length > 0;
const hasLeadForm = leadForm.title.trim().length > 0 && leadForm.lead.trim().length > 0;
const heroLayoutPreference =
  (hero as { layout?: HeroLayoutPreference } | null | undefined)?.layout
  ?? clientBrief.heroLayoutPreference
  ?? 'split';
const cardVariant = componentVariantMarkers.card;
const sectionVariant = componentVariantMarkers.section;
---
<MainLayout
  title={siteMeta.title}
  description={siteMeta.description}
  immersive={heroLayoutPreference === 'immersive' || heroLayoutPreference === 'fullscreen-visual'}
>
  {isBusinessContentReady && hasHero && hero && <Hero hero={hero} />}

  <div class:list={['page-surface', isBusinessContentReady && hasHero && heroLayoutPreference === 'immersive' && 'page-surface--overlap']}>
    <div class="page-surface__inner">
      {!isBusinessContentReady && (
        <section class:list={['section', sectionVariant.className]} id="content-pending" {...sectionVariant.dataAttrs}>
          <article class:list={['feature-card', cardVariant.className]} {...cardVariant.dataAttrs}>
            <p class="section-heading__eyebrow">Демо</p>
            <h1>Контент готовится</h1>
            <p>Публичная версия появится после наполнения клиентского контента.</p>
          </article>
        </section>
      )}

      {isBusinessContentReady && hasVisualCards && <VisualCardsSection title={visualCards.title} lead={visualCards.lead} items={visualCards.items} />}
      {isBusinessContentReady && hasServices && <ServicesSection title={services.title} lead={services.lead} items={services.items} />}
      {isBusinessContentReady && hasBenefits && <BenefitsSection title={benefits.title} lead={benefits.lead} items={benefits.items} />}
      {isBusinessContentReady && hasTrustProof && <TrustProof title={trustProof.title} lead={trustProof.lead} items={trustProof.items} />}
      {isBusinessContentReady && hasProcess && <ProcessSection title={process.title} lead={process.lead} steps={process.steps} />}
      {isBusinessContentReady && hasFaq && <Faq title={faq.title} lead={faq.lead} items={faq.items} />}
      {isBusinessContentReady && hasLeadForm && <LeadForm title={leadForm.title} lead={leadForm.lead} topics={leadForm.topics} />}
    </div>
  </div>
</MainLayout>

File: apps/site/README.md

# site

Astro public website frontend for this generated quick-start project.

Useful commands:
- cd apps/site
- npm install
  - `npm install` может молчать 20-60 секунд. Жди до 60 секунд и не прерывай команду раньше только из-за отсутствия вывода. Если через 60 секунд нет прогресса, проверь зависание/сеть/частично созданные зависимости и запиши это в `docs/conductor/run_log.md`.
- npm run finalize
- npm run preview

Publish-ready result:
- ../../public-demo/index.html

Source:
- src/data/client-brief.ts
- src/data/business-context.ts
- src/pages/index.astro
- src/data/landing.ts
- src/data/site.ts
- src/data/pages.ts
- src/components/*
- src/styles/site.css

================
File: docs/conductor/approval_matrix.md
================
# Approval Matrix

This file defines what needs human approval before an agent acts.

| Action | Default Level | Human Approval Required |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Read files and search the repo | L0 | No |
| Produce a plan | L1 | No |
| Edit approved files | L2 | Yes |
| Add dependencies | L2 | Yes |
| Change runtime configuration | L2 | Yes |
| Run local checks | L2 | Yes unless already approved |
| Create a branch or draft PR | L3 | Yes |
| Inspect or fix CI | L4 | Yes |
| Deploy | L5 | Always |
| Read or transmit secrets | Denied | Never |
| Destructive delete or history rewrite | Denied by default | Explicit one-off approval |

## Approval Must Name

- task id
- autonomy level
- allowed paths
- denied paths
- allowed commands
- required checks
- rollback plan when runtime behavior changes

================
File: docs/conductor/autonomy_levels.md
================
# Autonomy Levels

Autonomy increases gradually. The default level is `L2`.

## L0: Read Only

- inspect files
- search and summarize
- no edits

## L1: Plan Only

- inspect
- propose changes and checks
- no edits

## L2: Approved Bounded Implementation

- edit approved paths only after human approval
- run approved checks
- update docs and logs tied to the task

## L3: PR Preparation

- all L2 actions
- branch and draft PR preparation after approval

## L4: CI Fix

- inspect failing CI
- apply bounded fixes to the same approved task scope

## L5: Controlled Deploy

- run an explicitly approved deploy flow
- report deploy health or rollback status

## Always Denied Unless Explicitly Approved

- secrets exposure
- destructive history actions
- undeclared infra changes

================
File: docs/conductor/handoff_template.md
================
# Handoff Template

Task:
From:
To:
Autonomy level:
Status:

## Summary

What changed or what was discovered.

## Current State

- Branch:
- Dirty files:
- Completed checks:
- Failed or skipped checks:

File: docs/conductor/security_policy.md
================
# Conductor Security Policy

This file defines the hard safety boundary for humans and agents.

## Secrets

Never commit, print, summarize, or transmit:

- `.env`
- real API keys
- private keys
- production tokens
- database passwords
- webhook secrets

Document required variables in `.env.example` with safe placeholders only.

## Deploy

Deploy is manual by default.

Agents must not:

- deploy without explicit approval
- assume SSH users or server paths
- copy secret files by default
- hardcode production domains
- run ad hoc commands on production hosts

## Destructive Actions

Denied by default:

- recursive deletion
- force reset
- force push
- history rewrite
- destructive database operations without a rollback plan

## Scope Control

If a task needs a new path, command, dependency, or runtime requirement outside
the approved plan, stop and ask for approval.

## Logging

L2+ work must record:

- what changed
- why it changed
- commands run
- checks run or skipped
- remaining risks

File: docs/conductor/workflow.md
================
# Manual Conductor Workflow

This file defines the lifecycle of human-controlled implementation work.

It is the process layer.

It does not duplicate:

- approval details from `approval_matrix.md`
- autonomy details from `autonomy_levels.md`
- security rules from `security_policy.md`

## Default Operating Mode

The default mode is `L2` approved bounded implementation.

That means:

- inspect and planning may happen first
- file edits begin only after human approval of the task boundaries
- deploy, merge, secret handling, and destructive actions stay manual unless
  explicitly approved

## Lifecycle

1. Draft the task.
2. Inspect the repository or generated workspace.
3. Propose a bounded plan.
4. Get human approval for L2 implementation.
5. Implement only inside approved paths.
6. Run the agreed checks.
7. Update the run log.
8. Hand off for review, publish, or the next owner.

## Required Companion Docs

Every L2+ task should use:

- `task_template.md`
- `run_log_template.md`
- `approval_matrix.md`
- `autonomy_levels.md`
- `security_policy.md`

## Status Values

- `draft`
- `planned`
- `approved`
- `in_progress`
- `verifying`
- `blocked`
- `done`

## Rule

If approval boundaries are unclear, the task must stop before implementation.

# Agent Task Tree

## purpose

Working execution tree for a site task. This file tracks branch status and
short implementation notes. It does not replace `AGENT_TASK.md`,
`CLIENT_BRIEF.md`, `CONTENT_SEED_TASK.md`, `AGENT_LAUNCH.md`,
`EXECUTION_PLAN.md`, or `VALIDATION_RULES.md`.

## source of truth

- Business truth: `docs/AGENT_TASK.md`, `docs/CLIENT_BRIEF.md`, `docs/CONTENT_SEED_TASK.md`, and `docs/intake/*`
- Execution truth: `docs/EXECUTION_PLAN.md`, `docs/AGENT_GUARDRAILS.md`, and `docs/AGENT_VISUAL_STANDARD.md`
- Reference truth: `docs/AGENT_LAUNCH.md`
- Validation truth: `docs/VALIDATION_RULES.md`
- Map entry: `docs/maps/MAP_INDEX.md`
- Status log: `docs/conductor/run_log.md`
- Style direction: `docs/maps/STYLE_DIRECTION_MAP.md`

## request context

- Project type: `landing`
- Niche: `local-services`
- siteStructure: `home-only`
- futureGrowth: `demo-only`
- style: `dark-lime-creative`
- Enabled apps: `site`
- Presentation blocks:
  - benefits
  - reviews
  - cases
  - steps
- Business capabilities:
  - lead-form
  - faq

## map-driven cycle

Map -> Expand -> Implement -> Mark -> Report

## status legend

- todo
- doing
- done
- blocked
- skipped

## task tree

```text
site scaffold
  -> site structure [done]
  -> style direction [done]
  -> home page [done]
     -> header [done]
        -> desktop header [done]
        -> mobile compact header [done]
        -> burger behavior [done]
        -> drawer layout [done]
        -> drawer contrast [done]
        -> drawer CTA width [done]
        -> no horizontal overflow [done]
     -> hero [done]
     -> benefits / offer [done]
     -> products or services preview [done]
     -> trust / proof [done]
     -> lead form [done]
     -> footer [done]
```

## allowed updates

- status: todo / doing / done / blocked / skipped
- implementation note
- files touched
- blocked reason

## denied updates

- changing component requirements
- weakening acceptance criteria
- rewriting maps to fit incomplete code
- changing business intent

## allowed inference

- The agent may detail the current branch.
- The agent may choose the local technical implementation inside scope.
- The agent may add accessibility, focus, and mobile details.
- The agent may create local site components if that simplifies the code.

## denied inference

- Do not expand business scope.
- Do not add backend, API, payment, auth, or cart work when the brief does not require it.
- Do not invent reviews, awards, numbers, or real case studies.
- Do not touch deploy, infra, or SEO.

## reporting rule

After finishing each branch, update the status and leave a short implementation note:

- what was implemented
- files touched
- status: done / blocked / skipped
- if blocked: why

Example:

```text
header [done]
implementation note:
- Created responsive header with desktop nav and mobile drawer.
- Files touched: src/components/Header.*
- Burger closes on overlay, Esc, and nav link click.
```

## status

- Map status: `done`
- Project type: `landing`
- Page family: `landing`
- Site structure: `home-only`

## agent notes

- If a branch is too general, expand it in place before coding.
- Header work should be tracked on the listed sub-branches, not collapsed into a single `header done` note.
- Keep branch notes short and specific.

# Benefits Component Map

## purpose

Describe the offer / benefits block so the agent can turn the main value
proposition into a readable section with a clear conversion path.

## source of truth

- Business truth: `docs/AGENT_TASK.md`, `docs/CLIENT_BRIEF.md`, `docs/CONTENT_SEED_TASK.md`, and `docs/intake/*`
- Execution truth: `docs/EXECUTION_PLAN.md`, `docs/AGENT_GUARDRAILS.md`, and `docs/AGENT_VISUAL_STANDARD.md`
- Reference truth: `docs/AGENT_LAUNCH.md`
- Validation truth: `docs/VALIDATION_RULES.md`
- Map entry: `docs/maps/MAP_INDEX.md`

## map edit policy

This component map is read-only guidance for implementation.
Do not rewrite this map to match incomplete code.
If the implementation cannot satisfy this map, mark the related branch as blocked in `docs/maps/AGENT_TASK_TREE.md` and explain why in `docs/conductor/run_log.md`.

## request context

- Project type: `landing`
- Niche: `local-services`
- siteStructure: `home-only`
- futureGrowth: `demo-only`
- style: `dark-lime-creative`
- Enabled apps: `site`
- Presentation blocks:
  - benefits
  - reviews
  - cases
  - steps
- Business capabilities:
  - lead-form
  - faq

## tree

```text
benefits
  -> 3-6 benefits
  -> short headlines
  -> short explanations
  -> visual rhythm
  -> CTA connection
```

## required

- 3-6 benefits
- each benefit is tied to a client pain or gain
- short headlines
- clear descriptions
- visual rhythm: cards, list, icons, or grid
- block should support the CTA rather than distract from it

## behavior

- benefits should scan in 5-7 seconds
- copy should be compact and useful
- cards or list items should hold their shape on mobile
- the block should feel like part of the same story as hero and form
- if a benefit card needs a visual anchor, use the local demo asset pool before reaching for external imagery

## allowed inference

- Choose cards, list, or grid.
- Adapt the benefits to the niche.
- Add micro-icons if they do not break the style.
- Connect the block to the primary CTA.
- Prefer `product-1.webp` through `product-8.webp`, `category-1.webp` through `category-4.webp`, or `gallery-1.webp` through `gallery-4.webp` for compact card visuals. Use `image-1.webp`, `image-2.webp`, or `image-3.webp` only when the scaffold still exposes the legacy pool.

## denied inference

- Do not write “best on the market” without evidence.
- Do not invent guarantees.
- Do not add medical or legal promises.
- Do not make the cards too long.

## common failure cases

- benefits are too generic
- all cards feel the same and say nothing new
- text length breaks the grid
- mobile cards become too narrow
- there is no clear link to hero or form

## component/page acceptance

- the benefits are understandable in 5-7 seconds
- the grid does not break on mobile
- the block strengthens the offer instead of decorating the page

## status

- Map status: `draft`
- Page family: `landing`
- Niche: `local-services`
- CTA target: `send a request`

## agent notes

- If the brief is sparse, lead with pain-first benefits that stay honest.

# FAQ Component Map

## purpose

Describe a reusable FAQ block so the agent can answer common objections without
adding a separate custom HTML pattern for every page.

## source of truth

- Business truth: `docs/AGENT_TASK.md`, `docs/CLIENT_BRIEF.md`, `docs/CONTENT_SEED_TASK.md`, and `docs/intake/*`
- Execution truth: `docs/EXECUTION_PLAN.md`, `docs/AGENT_GUARDRAILS.md`, and `docs/AGENT_VISUAL_STANDARD.md`
- Reference truth: `docs/AGENT_LAUNCH.md`
- Validation truth: `docs/VALIDATION_RULES.md`
- Map entry: `docs/maps/MAP_INDEX.md`
- UI contract truth: `.botweaver/pipeline/spec.json` and `.botweaver/pipeline/launch-instruction.json` via `ui_contracts.faq_icon`.
- FAQ source lives in `apps/site/src/components/Faq.astro`; FAQ items belong in `src/data/site.ts` or `src/data/pages.ts`.
- Landing starter FAQ lives in `apps/site/src/components/Faq.astro` with items in `src/data/landing.ts`.

## map edit policy

This component map is read-only guidance for implementation.
Do not rewrite this map to match incomplete code.
If the implementation cannot satisfy this map, mark the related branch as blocked in `docs/maps/AGENT_TASK_TREE.md` and explain why in `docs/conductor/run_log.md`.

## request context

- Project type: `landing`
- Niche: `local-services`
- siteStructure: `home-only`
- futureGrowth: `demo-only`
- style: `dark-lime-creative`
- Enabled apps: `site`
- Presentation blocks:
  - benefits
  - reviews
  - cases
  - steps
- Business capabilities:
  - lead-form
  - faq

## tree

```text
faq
  -> question
  -> answer
  -> reusable disclosure pattern
  -> mobile-safe spacing
```

## required

- 3-6 common questions or objections
- concise answers
- reusable disclosure pattern
- native `<details>/<summary>` by default
- accessible toggle states if disclosure is interactive
- visible focus states
- line-based disclosure icon instead of raw text glyphs
- light open/close polish with CSS transitions or animation evidence
- data source: `src/data/site.ts` or `src/data/pages.ts`
- FAQ icon must follow `ui_contracts.faq_icon`; scaffold/validator v1 currently supports only `css-line`.

## behavior

- questions should be easy to scan
- answers should be short enough to keep the page moving
- the pattern should work on mobile without clipping or overflow
- open/close behavior should feel polished rather than abrupt
- disclosure icon should feel intentional and not look like a pasted text character
- future-reserved FAQ icon names such as `svg` or `chevron` are not a signal to invent new icon systems in v1
- if the block needs defaults, keep them honest and specific to the request

## allowed inference

- Use native `<details>` / `<summary>` by default or a small accessible accordion only when needed.
- Keep the answers specific to the request and business niche.
- Add a light CTA bridge after the FAQ if it helps conversion.
- Draw the disclosure icon with CSS lines, for example through `summary::after` with two `linear-gradient` strokes or an equivalent line-based icon treatment, because v1 canonical support is `css-line`.
- Add lightweight CSS polish such as `grid-template-rows`, `max-height`, `opacity`, `transform`, marker rotation, or summary/background transitions.

## denied inference

- Do not turn FAQ into a long marketing article.
- Do not invent guarantees or hidden process claims.
- Do not make the block depend on a custom backend.
- Do not use a raw text disclosure marker such as `content: "+"`.
- Do not implement `svg` or `chevron` FAQ icon variants in scaffold/validator v1.
- Do not ship a raw disclosure block with no focus states or no motion/polish at all.
- Do not add a heavy JS accordion or animation library for the default scaffold.

## common failure cases

- answers are too long
- accordion controls are not accessible
- disclosure icon is a raw `+` text glyph
- FAQ becomes a text dump
- mobile spacing feels cramped
- FAQ opens abruptly with no visual polish

## component/page acceptance

- The FAQ block is reusable.
- Questions and answers are clear.
- The block does not feel like a dumping ground for missing content.
- The FAQ uses native disclosure, the v1 `css-line` icon contract, and lightweight CSS polish.

## status

- Map status: `draft`
- Page family: `landing`
- CTA target: `send a request`

## agent notes

- Keep the FAQ short, honest, and easy to reuse on any site page.
